<script type="text/javascript">
	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<a tabindex="-1" id="job_header"></a>
<div data-tn-component="jobHeader">
<b class="jobtitle"><font size="+1">VP of Engineering</font></b>

<br>
<span class="company">IntelliPower Inc</span>
     -
<span class="location">Orange, CA 92865</span>
    </div>
    <table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 border=0><tr><td class="snip">
<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>Position Summary: </b></p><p>The Vice President of Engineering manages the Development and Support of advanced technology Uninterruptible Power Systems, Power Conversion Systems and Power Control Systems for military and industrial applications where high reliability in harsh environments is required. Provides expert technical leadership for power electronics and embedded software to the team.</p><p><b>Requirements and Duties: </b></p><ul><li>Must have successful hands-on experiences with the design of all aspects of UPS and power conversion products using advanced state-of-the-art technology with focus on digital embedded DSP system controls.</li><li>Emphasis is on high level of technical competence with innovative circuit design, firmware design and systems design based upon strong history of product design successes.</li><li>Current projects include the completion of very flexible high frequency isolated UPS product release using total digital DSP control and paralleling of AC UPSs with N+1 redundancy. Company has a continuous stream of large and small development projects including.</li><li>Requirements are for the successful candidate to have experiences with a wide range of high frequency based power conversion topologies for DC-DC converters, Single & 3-phase Power Factor Correctors, Inverters, Chargers, etc. and with the integration of embedded microcontroller and DSP support systems for the most efficient hardware and firmware control for integrated products.</li><li>Requires experiences with embedded microcontroller circuitry designs, communications interface designs and embedded software control systems including paralleling of inverters for AC output UPS systems in an N+1 redundancy environment.</li><li>Must be able to design circuits and integrated systems to achieve very highly reliable and cost effective power conversion products for volume production.</li><li>Must be able to direct the layout of design circuit boards to achieve noise free products efficiently to move products to producible state in short time frames.</li><li>EMC and magnetics design experiences are required.</li><li>15 to 20 years closely related experience with UPS designing and DSP digitally controls product implementation.</li><li>Must be able to prioritize work load and work in a multitasking small company fast track environment.</li><li>Strong communication and documentation skills are required</li></ul><p><b>Education: </b></p><ul><li>Management and leadership training</li><li>Bachelors Degree in a relevant Engineering discipline, required</li><li>Advanced Degree in Power Electronics Engineering and Advanced Control Systems, preferred</li></ul><p><b>Skills and Abilities: </b></p><ul><li>Proven hands on experience as required for managing development teams in a fast track high growth technology company environment.</li><li>Proven ability to manage and motivate a diverse engineering development team to achieve excellent engineering designs meeting aggressive schedules.</li><li>The ability to communicate verbally and in writing with the Engineering Team, the CEO and other members of the Top Management Team with full transparency</li><li>Must be able to prioritize work load in a multitasking and active growth environment with positive It Can Be Done motivation skills.</li><li>Must be able to work independently with minimum supervision and have the ability to interact positively with others including the CEO and Management Team.</li><li>Proven ability to achieve assigned goals and to flow down written goals to the Engineering Team members with appropriate over sight to ensure successful achievement.</li><li>Excellent verbal and written communication skills.</li><li>Proficient in computer related tools.</li><li>Very strong work ethic with determination and focus to achieve challenging goals. Willingness to work a flexible schedule</li></ul><p><i>EOE/Minorities/Females/Veterans/Disabled</i></p><p><i>All applicants will receive consideration for employments without regard to race, color, creed, religion, national origin,sex, sexual orientation, disability, age, marital status, status with regard to genetic information or any other characteristic protected by applicable Federal, State or Local laws.</i></p><p><b>About IntelliPower: </b></p><p>Since 1988, IntelliPower, a profitable growing privately-held corporation, designs, develops, manufactures and supports high performance, rugged, specially-configured Uninterruptible Power Systems (UPS), Power Conditioners, Frequency / Power Converters. Markets include industry-leading OEMs, Systems Integrators and major users for mission critical military, industrial and commercial applications. IntelliPowers major strengths include supplying high reliability power protection and conversion solutions for harsh environment supported by excellent support services. Our solutions exactly meet all of our customers requirements. IntelliPower has become the leader in supplying rugged power solutions for military and industrial harsh environment applications and is continuing to grow by increasing market share.</p><p>IntelliPowers client list includes: General Dynamics, Northrop Grumman, Lockheed Martin, Cubic Defense Systems, SAIC, BAE, Raytheon, L3 Communications, National Oil Well Varco (NOV), Caprock Communications, Weatherford International, Halliburton, Schlumberger, all branches of the United States Military, and other industrial and commercial users. IntelliPower has won far more military programs than any other UPS company including very large programs such as the Navy CANES Program and the SEWIP Program, the Army CHS/Win-T Programs and the US Marines DDS-M Program. Maximum focus is placed on complete customer satisfaction at all times. General Dynamics and US Army have honored IntelliPower with their Outstanding Industry Partner Award for Excellence, 2014 Defender of the Year and 2106 Defender of the Year. Web site is: www.intellipower.com.</p><p>Rather than only offering a selection of fixed function models, IntelliPower has earned an outstanding reputation as the leader in the design and development of rugged multifunction UPS System and Power Conversion System features specifically tailored to the clients individual criteria to protect mission-critical applications in specific environments and operating with worldwide power</p><p>sources. All IntelliPower rugged power conversion products are designed and configured using internally developed electronics hardware and firmware technology. Moreover, our ability to provide timely and competent hands-on, support services, as well as engineering responsiveness and flexible manufacturing options have helped us become the industry leader in Uninterruptible Power Supplies for challenging harsh electrical and physical environments.</p><p>IntelliPower operates fully with its ISO 9001:2008 based QMS System, now moving to ISO 9001: 2015, covering all aspects of our business with heavy focus on Continuous Improvement. Our dedication to the highest standards of product development reliability and commitment to complete customer satisfaction has resulted in a very growth rates gaining new customers. IntelliPower has a very strong financial balance sheet with no debt and consistent high profitability allowing us to support major projects and high volume production of specialized products.</p><p>Please submit resume, references and salary history with your application.</p><p>Job Type: Full-time</p><p>Job Location:</p><ul><li>Orange, CA</li></ul><p>Required education:</p><ul><li>Bachelor's</li></ul><p>Required experience:</p><ul><li>Power Electronics Engineering: 10 years</li><li>Sr Engineering Management: 10 years</li><li>EMC and magnetics design: 5 years</li><li>power conversion: 10 years</li><li>embedded microcontroller circuitry: 5 years</li></ul></span><br><div id="p_154cc661d8de3a89">
<div class="result-link-bar-container result-link-bar-viewjob">

    <header class="pf-rc-pageheading clearfix">
    	
    	<span class="bread-crumbs"><span>Job Opportunity</span></span>
    </header>
	<section class="pf-rc-component">
            <div class="job"><div class="details"><div class="header"><h3 class="title">Electrical Engineer - CCA Designer</h3>&nbsp;<span class="other-info"><span>10/2/17</span><span>--Electrical</span><span>USA - CA - Van Nuys</span></span></div></div></div>
    </section>
    <section class="pf-rc-component">
            <div class="button-row fixed clearfix">
		
            	<div class="button">
                 	<A id='Refer__a' HREF='res_referafriend.html' title='Refer This Job to a Friend' class="btn" id="referafriend">Refer</A>
                </div>
		
		
                
	            
	                <div class="button">
	                	<A id='Save__a' HREF='res_savetosavedjoblist.html?page=er-res_viewjob&erjob=62532' class="btn" id="save">Save</A>
	                </div>
	            
            	
					<div class="button">
	                	<A id='Apply__a' HREF='startsubmission.html?erjob=62532' class="btn primary" id="apply">Apply</A>
	                </div>
	            
	            
	            
	            
            </div>
            <hr>
            
	        
            <h4><span>Job ID:</span>&nbsp;ES20170210-21131</h4>
            

            <h4>Description:</h4>
            <div>
            	<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Title:</strong>&nbsp;Electrical Engineer - CCA Designer</span><br /><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>REQ ID:&nbsp;</strong>ES20170210-21131</span><br /><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Location:</strong> Van Nuys, California</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Job Description:</strong></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Responsible for the digital CCA design process including requirements generation, preliminary design, peer reviews, detailed design, test plan generation, and integration and test</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Understand the requirements and architect a digital CCA solution including the use of TI DSP processors, Freescale or Intel Processors, Microcontrollers, FPGA(Xilinx, Altera&hellip;), CPLD, and volatile/no-volatile memory (DDRx, SRAM, ROM, Flash&hellip;) components</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Design high speed memory interfaces (DDRx)</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">High speed serial designs and protocols (PCIe/Gen3 PCIe, SRIO&hellip;)</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Work with board technologies such as HDI, Meg6, and back drilling</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Utilize RF simulation tool ADS to characterize high speed board routing</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Utilize the Cadence software suite used to generate the circuit card designs (Schematic Capture, Constraint-Driven, Layout, Simulation, and Timing Analysis)</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Work in a team environment and negotiate solutions with Hardware / Software Engineering and Systems Engineering&nbsp;</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Work independently with strong technical leadership in generating the digital CCA design solutions and support the complete testing and qualification of the deliverable system</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Qualifications:</strong></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">BS Degree in electrical/computer engineering and&nbsp;10+ years or related experience</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Preferred/Additional Skills</strong>:</span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">DoD Secret security clearance</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience with Avionics designs</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience with high speed serial protocols Ethernet and Fibre Channel network protocols</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience designing 10G Ethernet based Network Interface or 10G Ethernet Switch designs</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience designing and understanding of IPV4 or IPV6</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience with design for test and design for manufacturability techniques</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Experience using Cadence Incisive Enterprise Simulator, Subversion, Python or Perl</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Understanding&nbsp;of efficiency metrics such as hours/schematic page (Productivity and Quality)</span></li>
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">Ability to write C++ and use Microsoft Visual Studio</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><strong>Security Clearance: </strong></span></p>
<ul type="disc">
<li><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;">This position requires the candidate to possess or have the ability to obtain a DoD Secret security clearance. In order to obtain a clearance you need to be a US Citizen and show proof of citizenship.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><em>Harris is an Equal Opportunity/Affirmative Action Employer. We consider applicants without regard to race, color, religion, age, national origin, ancestry, ethnicity, gender, gender identity, gender expression, sexual orientation, marital status, veteran status, disability, genetic information, citizenship status, or membership in any other group protected by federal, state or local law.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: verdana, geneva; font-size: 14px;"><em>By submitting your r&eacute;sum&eacute; for this position, you understand and agree that Harris Corporation may share your r&eacute;sum&eacute;, as well as any other related personal information or documentation you provide, with its subsidiaries and affiliated companies for the purpose of considering you for other available positions.</em></span></p>
            </div>

    else {
      // We were able to render this page, but we don't have an iPaaS Session
      jQuery.get("logout.html?defer=true");
      window.iPaaS.signOff();
    }
    window.iPaaS.sessionEnded = function () {
      // Make an ajax request to logout.html?defer=true
      jQuery.get("logout.html?defer=true");
      window.iPaaS.signOff();
    };

  }
  if ( window.iPaaS ) {
    window.iPaaS.ready(handleSessions);
  }
</script>
    </body>

    </html>

                       globals: false, callback: window.map_init_basic};

  // Display the map centered on the job location
  function map_init_basic(jobMap) {
    jobMap.off();
    jobMap.remove();
    geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
    var address = 'Irvine, CA, USA';
    geocoder.geocode({ 'address': address }, function (results, status) {
      if (status === google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
        coordinates = results[0].geometry.location;
        var latLngArray = new L.LatLng(coordinates.lat(), coordinates.lng());
        jobMap = new L.Map('map', { center: latLngArray, zoom: 14 });
        var marker = new L.marker(latLngArray).addTo(jobMap);
        var googleLayer = new L.Google('ROADMAP');
        jobMap.addLayer(googleLayer);
      }
    });
    new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(document.getElementById('id_address'), {types: ['geocode']});
  }

  // Update the label of the file inputs when a new file is uploaded
  $('.inputfile').each(function() {
    $(this).find('input').on('change', function(e) {
      var $parent = $(this).closest('.inputfile');
      var fileName = e.target.value.split('\\').pop();
      if (fileName) {
        $parent.find('.inputfile__filename').html(fileName);
        $parent.find('.inputfile__download-link').remove();
      }
    });
  });
</script>

                <p>
                    <div class="section-data" data-section="1"><!--START_SECTION_1-->Senior Firmware Engineer needed for growing R&D team in Torrance! Linux, ARM Cortex, Micro Controllers, Embedded Systems, C/C++, TCP/IP<br><br>Embedded Software Engineer needed for a growing team in Torrance.  This position is part of the R&D organizations software engineering team developing new products and supporting existing products. The ideal candidate will collaborate with the other team members on the development  of software and its integration with production-line products which include real time embedded systems.<br><br>Our products are used the final stages of the manufacturing process and use modern technologies like computer vision on the assembly line to investigate product issues, quality control and adhere to standards. We have customers - companies and brands that rival Coca Cola who use our devices regularly throughout their packaging process. <br><br>Do you live craft beer? Our products are used heavily in the modern craft beer craze as well.<!--END_SECTION_1--></div><h4 class="section-title">Top Reasons to Work with Us</h4><div class="section-data section-data-title" data-section="2"><!--START_SECTION_2-->1. Be a part of a market leading yet still growing organization who is bringing their entire engineering team in house!<br>2. Have the ability to shape the culture and development process for new team and product!<br>3. Competitive salary and benefit package offered!<!--END_SECTION_2--></div><h4 class="section-title">What You Will Be Doing</h4><div class="section-data section-data-title" data-section="5"><!--START_SECTION_5-->- Develop real-time embedded software in C/C++ <br>- Produce design documentation <br>- Integrate and debug software on test machines <br>- Develop test code and test automation scripts <br>- Track revisions and log defects using the filtec software development process<!--END_SECTION_5--></div><h4 class="section-title">What You Need for this Position</h4><div class="section-data section-data-title" data-section="7"><!--START_SECTION_7-->- Strong firmware development experience<br>- Experience with ARM Cortex and ARM Controllers<br>- KEIL embedded development tools expeirence / Microcontroller Development kit / MDK<br>- 3+ years of software design experience working with C and C++ <br>- Embedded micro-controller applications<br>- Familiarity with 8051 and Arm based systems / micro-controller architectures, desirable.<br>- Communications protocols, RS232 & TCP/IP<!--END_SECTION_7--></div><h4 class="section-title">What's In It for You</h4><div class="section-data section-data-title" data-section="8"><!--START_SECTION_8-->Strong base salary + total comp<br>Solid Health Benefits + PTO Plan<br>Lots of upward mobibility<br>Working with a smaller team and company with lots of visibility and ability to affect the product<br>You can be a bigger fish in a smaller pond<br>Location right in Torrance - potentially a great commute for some folks who have drive far for work<br>Stable, viable and growing product that's becoming a leader in a niche space<!--END_SECTION_8--></div><div class="section-data" data-section="9"><!--START_SECTION_9-->So, if you are a Senior Firmware Engineer - with good C/C++ and KEIL / ARM Cortex development experience, please apply today!<!--END_SECTION_9--></div>
                </p>

                    <p>Applicants must be authorized to work in the U.S.</p>

		<div class="descriptionWrapper">
			<div class="jobDescription"><span itemprop="description"><h1><strong>Software Engineer</strong></h1>Our vision is beyond a connected home, rather a smarter home where technology is your friend and not an obstacle. Our fantastic team is focused on next generation distributed platforms for the connected home ecosystem; we solve real life problems and bring improvements to the masses. We are infatuated by technology; however only see it as the means and not the goal itself. We accept no boundaries and no problem should remain unresolved.<br /><br />Our products and technologies are touched by well over 250 million people every week, and were just getting started! We design & developed an extraordinary number of products for the connected home, backed by a complete ecosystem ofdata driven software solutions & cloud servicesfor connected devices from leading brands in mobile, gaming and consumer electronics segments!<br /><br /><span style=font-size:16pt;><strong>Development projects will vary based on new product development, complexity and product lines. This team creates innovative software that runs on top of our firmware. Technologies will range from Android to C++ to Python to Firmware.</strong></span><h1><span style=font-size:14pt;>Responsibilities</span></h1><ul> <li>Design and develop firmware and software for innovative and highly-optimized connected controllers and sensors.</li> <li>Continuously improve our development process.</li> <li>Write design documentation.</li> <li>Evaluate and integrate software from 3<sup>rd</sup> party vendors.</li> <li>Review designs and source code from other developers.</li></ul><h2>Requirements</h2><ul> <li>Self-motivated, innovative and persistent; problem solver who does not accept failure.</li> <li>BSc in Computer Science, Software Engineering or Electrical Engineering with a very strong software component and +10 years of relevant experience; MSc preferred.</li> <li>Great team player with great interpersonal skills.</li> <li>Experience in C programming on severely resource-constrained platforms.</li> <li>Knowledge of microcontroller architectures.</li> <li>Experience with object-oriented design principles.</li> <li>Experience developing on a bare device and using an RTOS.</li> <li>Experience designing device drivers for peripherals like external memories and sensors.</li> <li>Experience with power-management.</li> <li>Experience using debuggers, logic analyzers and oscilloscopes.</li> <li>Experience with consumer IR and RF protocols, including ZigBee, RF4CE, Wi-Fi, Bluetooth Classic and Smart is a strong plus.</li> <li>Knowledge of digital and analog circuit design is a plus.</li></ul><br /></span></div>
